If I enable punctuation, f.e by clicking on button "punctuation", then refresh the page, punctuation is disabled. All other configs are retained (f.e change time from 30 to 60 and refresh, etc).

### Expected Behavior

Should retain punctuation. Was working couple weeks ago like this.

### Steps To Reproduce

1. Open https://monkeytype.com/
2. Click on punctuation
3. Hit page refresh (F5)

### Environment

- OS: Linux/Windows
- Browser: Edge/Firefox
- Browser Version: (only have Edge ATM) - 137.0.3296.68



### Anything else?

I do see that "config" in local storage changes to `"punctuation": true` when I enable it, but refreshing the page changes that back to false. The same happens with "numbers".

I take it that these values are both booleans and javascript has a nasty habit of transforming "undefined" and "null" into boolean as `false` without being told. I'd assume that at some point there is a bit of code that reads configs from db or url or somewhere else where neither "punctuation" nor "numbers" are saved and then transforms their values to false and uses that for test (and storing to local storage).

   100	}
   101	
   102	export function genericSet<T extends keyof ConfigSchemas.Config>(
   103	  key: T,
   104	  value: ConfigSchemas.Config[T],
   105	  nosave: boolean = false
   106	): boolean {
   107	  const metadata = configMetadata[key] as ConfigMetadataObject[T];
   108	  if (metadata === undefined) {
   109	    throw new Error(`Config metadata for key "${key}" is not defined.`);
   110	  }
   111	
   112	  if (metadata.overrideValue) {
   113	    value = metadata.overrideValue({
   114	      value,
   115	      currentValue: config[key],
   116	      currentConfig: config,
   117	    });
   118	  }
   119	
   120	  const previousValue = config[key];
   121	
   122	  if (
   123	    metadata.changeRequiresRestart &&
   124	    TestState.isActive &&
   125	    config.funbox.includes("no_quit")
   126	  ) {
   127	    Notifications.add("No quit funbox is active. Please finish the test.", 0, {
   128	      important: true,
   129	    });
   130	    console.warn(
   131	      `Could not set config key "${key}" with value "${JSON.stringify(
   132	        value
   133	      )}" - no quit funbox active.`
   134	    );
   135	    return false;
   136	  }
   137	
   138	  if (metadata.isBlocked?.({ value, currentConfig: config })) {
   139	    console.warn(
   140	      `Could not set config key "${key}" with value "${JSON.stringify(
   141	        value
   142	      )}" - blocked.`
   143	    );
   144	    return false;
   145	  }
   146	
   147	  const schema = ConfigSchemas.ConfigSchema.shape[key] as ZodSchema;
   148	
   149	  if (!isConfigValueValid(metadata.displayString ?? key, value, schema)) {
   150	    console.warn(
   151	      `Could not set config key "${key}" with value "${JSON.stringify(
   152	        value
   153	      )}" - invalid value.`
   154	    );
   155	    return false;
   156	  }
   157	
   158	  if (!canSetConfigWithCurrentFunboxes(key, value, config.funbox)) {
   159	    console.warn(
   160	      `Could not set config key "${key}" with value "${JSON.stringify(
   161	        value
   162	      )}" - funbox conflict.`
   163	    );
   164	    return false;
   165	  }
   166	
   167	  if (metadata.overrideConfig) {
   168	    const targetConfig = metadata.overrideConfig({
   169	      value,
   170	      currentConfig: config,
   171	    });
   172	
   173	    for (const targetKey of typedKeys(targetConfig)) {
   174	      const targetValue = targetConfig[
   175	        targetKey
   176	      ] as ConfigSchemas.Config[keyof typeof configMetadata];
   177	
   178	      if (config[targetKey] === targetValue) {
   179	        continue; // no need to set if the value is already the same
   180	      }
   181	
   182	      const set = genericSet(targetKey, targetValue, true);
   183	      if (!set) {
   184	        throw new Error(
   185	          `Failed to set config key "${targetKey}" with value "${targetValue}" for ${metadata.displayString} config override.`
   186	        );
   187	      }
   188	    }
   189	  }
   190	
   191	  config[key] = value;
   192	  if (!nosave) saveToLocalStorage(key, nosave);
   193	  ConfigEvent.dispatch(key, value, nosave, previousValue);
   194	
   195	  if (metadata.triggerResize && !nosave) {
   196	    triggerResize();
   197	  }
   198	
   199	  metadata.afterSet?.({ nosave: nosave || false, currentConfig: config });
   200

   885	export async function loadFromLocalStorage(): Promise<void> {
   886	  console.log("loading localStorage config");
   887	  const newConfig = configLS.get();
   888	  if (newConfig === undefined) {
   889	    await reset();
   890	  } else {
   891	    await apply(newConfig, true);
   892	    saveFullConfigToLocalStorage(true);
   893	  }
   894	  loadDone();
   895	}
   896	
   897	export function getConfigChanges(): Partial<Config> {
   898	  const configChanges: Partial<Config> = {};
   899	  typedKeys(config)
   900	    .filter((key) => {
   901	      return config[key] !== getDefaultConfig()[key];
   902	    })
   903	    .forEach((key) => {
   904	      //@ts-expect-error this is fine
   905	      configChanges[key] = config[key];
   906	    });
   907	  return configChanges;
   908	}
   909	
   910	export async function applyFromJson(json: string): Promise<void> {
   911	  try {
   912	    const parsedConfig = parseJsonWithSchema(
   913	      json,
   914	      ConfigSchemas.PartialConfigSchema.strip(),
   915	      {
   916	        migrate: (value) => {
   917	          if (Array.isArray(value)) {
   918	            throw new Error("Invalid config");
   919	          }
   920	          return migrateConfig(value);
   921	        },
   922	      }
   923	    );
   924	    await apply(parsedConfig, true);
   925	    saveFullConfigToLocalStorage();
   926	    Notifications.add("Done", 1);
   927	  } catch (e) {
   928	    const msg = createErrorMessage(e, "Failed to import settings");
   929	    console.error(msg);
   930	    Notifications.add(msg, -1);
   931	  }
   932	}

   822	export async function apply(
   823	  configToApply: Config | Partial<Config>,
   824	  fullReset = false
   825	): Promise<void> {
   826	  if (configToApply === undefined || configToApply === null) return;
   827	
   828	  //remove additional keys, migrate old values if needed
   829	  configToApply = sanitizeConfig(replaceLegacyValues(configToApply));
   830	
   831	  ConfigEvent.dispatch("fullConfigChange");
   832	
   833	  const defaultConfig = getDefaultConfig();
   834	  for (const key of typedKeys(fullReset ? defaultConfig : configToApply)) {
   835	    //@ts-expect-error this is fine, both are of type config
   836	    config[key] = defaultConfig[key];
   837	  }
   838	
   839	  const partialKeys = typedKeys(configToApply);
   840	  const partialKeysToApplyFirst = partialKeys.filter(
   841	    (key) => !lastConfigsToApply.has(key)
   842	  );
   843	  const partialKeysToApplyLast = Array.from(lastConfigsToApply.values()).filter(
   844	    (key) => partialKeys.includes(key)
   845	  );
   846	  const partialKeysToApply = [
   847	    ...partialKeysToApplyFirst,
   848	    ...partialKeysToApplyLast,
   849	  ];
   850	
   851	  const configKeysToReset: (keyof Config)[] = [];
   852	
   853	  for (const configKey of partialKeysToApply) {
   854	    const configValue = configToApply[
   855	      configKey
   856	    ] as ConfigSchemas.Config[keyof Config];
   857	
   858	    const set = genericSet(configKey, configValue, true);
   859	
   860	    if (!set) {
   861	      configKeysToReset.push(configKey);
   862	    }
   863	  }
   864	
   865	  for (const key of configKeysToReset) {
   866	    saveToLocalStorage(key);
   867	  }
   868	
   869	  ConfigEvent.dispatch(
   870	    "configApplied",
   871	    undefined,
   872	    undefined,
   873	    undefined,
   874	    config
   875	  );
   876	  ConfigEvent.dispatch("fullConfigChangeFinished");
   877	}
   878	
   879	export async function reset(): Promise<void> {
   880	  await apply(getDefaultConfig());
   881	  await DB.resetConfig();
   882	  saveFullConfigToLocalStorage(true);
   883	}

     9	import { getDefaultConfig } from "../constants/default-config";
    10	/**
    11	 * migrates possible outdated config and merges with the default config values
    12	 * @param config partial or possible outdated config
    13	 * @returns
    14	 */
    15	export function migrateConfig(config: PartialConfig | object): Config {
    16	  return mergeWithDefaultConfig(sanitizeConfig(replaceLegacyValues(config)));
    17	}
    18	
    19	function mergeWithDefaultConfig(config: PartialConfig): Config {
    20	  const defaultConfig = getDefaultConfig();
    21	  const mergedConfig = {} as Config;
    22	  for (const key of typedKeys(defaultConfig)) {
    23	    const newValue = config[key] ?? (defaultConfig[key] as ConfigValue);
    24	    //@ts-expect-error cant be bothered to deal with this
    25	    mergedConfig[key] = newValue;
    26	  }
    27	  return mergedConfig;
    28	}
    29	
    30	/**
    31	 * remove all values from the config which are not valid
    32	 */
    33	export function sanitizeConfig(
    34	  config: ConfigSchemas.PartialConfig
    35	): ConfigSchemas.PartialConfig {
    36	  //make sure to use strip()
    37	  return sanitize(ConfigSchemas.PartialConfigSchema.strip(), config);
    38	}

   180	  ) {
   181	    // migrate existing configs missing sub alt color
   182	    const colors = configObj.customThemeColors;
   183	    colors.splice(4, 0, "#000000");
   184	    configObj.customThemeColors = colors;
   185	  }
   186	
   187	  if (
   188	    Array.isArray(configObj.customBackgroundFilter) &&
   189	    //@ts-expect-error legacy configs
   190	    configObj.customBackgroundFilter.length === 5
   191	  ) {
   192	    const arr = configObj.customBackgroundFilter;
   193	    configObj.customBackgroundFilter = [arr[0], arr[1], arr[2], arr[3]];
   194	  }
   195	
   196	  if (typeof configObj.quoteLength === "number") {
   197	    if (configObj.quoteLength === -1) {
   198	      configObj.quoteLength = [0, 1, 2, 3];
   199	    } else {
   200	      configObj.quoteLength = [configObj.quoteLength];
   201	    }
   202	  }
   203	
   204	  if (configObj.tapeMargin !== undefined) {
   205	    if (configObj.tapeMargin < 10) {
   206	      configObj.tapeMargin = 10;
   207	    } else if (configObj.tapeMargin > 90) {
   208	      configObj.tapeMargin = 90;
   209	    }
   210	  }
   211	
   212	  if (configObj.maxLineWidth !== undefined) {
   213	    if (configObj.maxLineWidth < 20 && configObj.maxLineWidth !== 0) {
   214	      configObj.maxLineWidth = 20;
   215	    } else if (configObj.maxLineWidth > 1000) {
   216	      configObj.maxLineWidth = 1000;
   217	    }
   218	  }
   219	
   220	  return configObj;
   221	}
   222

    32	  public get(): T {
    33	    if (this.cache !== undefined) {
    34	      console.debug(`LS ${this.key} Got cached value:`, this.cache);
    35	      return this.cache;
    36	    }
    37	
    38	    console.debug(`LS ${this.key} Getting value from localStorage`);
    39	    const value = window.localStorage.getItem(this.key);
    40	
    41	    if (value === null) {
    42	      console.debug(`LS ${this.key} No value found, returning fallback`);
    43	      this.cache = this.fallback;
    44	      return this.cache;
    45	    }
    46	
    47	    let migrated = false;
    48	    const { data: parsed, error } = tryCatchSync(() =>
    49	      parseJsonWithSchema(value, this.schema, {
    50	        fallback: this.fallback,
    51	        migrate: (oldData, zodIssues) => {
    52	          console.debug(`LS ${this.key} Schema validation failed`);
    53	          migrated = true;
    54	          if (this.migrate) {
    55	            console.debug(
    56	              `LS ${this.key} Migrating from old format to new format`
    57	            );
    58	            this.cache = this.migrate(oldData, zodIssues);
    59	            return this.cache;
    60	          } else {
    61	            console.debug(
    62	              `LS ${this.key} No migration function provided, returning fallback`
    63	            );
    64	            this.cache = this.fallback;
    65	            return this.cache;
    66	          }
    67	        },
    68	      })
    69	    );
    70	
    71	    if (error) {
    72	      console.error(
    73	        `LS ${this.key} Failed to parse from localStorage: ${error.message}`
    74	      );
    75	      window.localStorage.setItem(this.key, JSON.stringify(this.fallback));
    76	      this.cache = this.fallback;
    77	      return this.cache;
    78	    }
    79	
    80	    if (migrated || parsed === this.fallback) {
    81	      console.debug(`LS ${this.key} Setting in localStorage`);
    82	      window.localStorage.setItem(this.key, JSON.stringify(parsed));
    83	    }
    84	
    85	    console.debug(`LS ${this.key} Got value:`, parsed);
    86	    this.cache = parsed;
    87	    return this.cache;
    88	  }
    89	
    90	  public set(data: T): boolean {
    91	    try {
    92	      console.debug(`LS ${this.key} Parsing to set in localStorage`);
    93	      const parsed = this.schema.parse(data);
    94	      console.debug(`LS ${this.key} Setting in localStorage`);
    95	      window.localStorage.setItem(this.key, JSON.stringify(parsed));
    96	      this.cache = parsed;
    97	      return true;
    98	    } catch (e) {
    99	      let message = "Unknown error occurred";
   100	
   101	      if (isZodError(e)) {
   102	        console.error(e);
   103	        // message = e.issues
   104	        //   .map((i) => (i.message ? i.message : JSON.stringify(i)))
   105	        //   .join(", ");
   106	        message = "Schema validation failed";
   107	      } else {
   108	        if ((e as Error).message.includes("exceeded the quota")) {
   109	          message =
   110	            "Local storage is full. Please clear some space and try again.";
   111	        }
   112	      }
   113	
   114	      const msg = `Failed to set ${this.key} in localStorage: ${message}`;
   115	      console.error(msg);
   116	      Notifications.add(msg, -1);
   117	
   118	      return false;
   119	    }
   120	  }
   121	}
   122

import { apply, __testing } from "./frontend/src/ts/config";
import { getDefaultConfig } from "./frontend/src/ts/constants/default-config";

async function reproduce() {
    const { replaceConfig, getConfig } = __testing;

    // 1. Initial state (default config)
    replaceConfig(getDefaultConfig());
    console.log("Initial punctuation:", getConfig().punctuation); // should be false

    // 2. Set punctuation to true
    // Mimic clicking punctuation button which calls genericSet("punctuation", true)
    // In our test, we'"'"'ll use apply to simulate loading from storage or just set it
    await apply({ punctuation: true }, false);
    console.log("Punctuation after setting:", getConfig().punctuation); // should be true

    // 3. Simulate page refresh/load from local storage
    const currentConfig = { ...getConfig() };
    console.log("Simulating refresh with config:", JSON.stringify({punctuation: currentConfig.punctuation, mode: currentConfig.mode}));
    
    // reset current config to default to simulate fresh start
    replaceConfig(getDefaultConfig());
    console.log("Config reset. Punctuation:", getConfig().punctuation);

    // Now apply the config we "saved"
    await apply(currentConfig, true);
    console.log("Punctuation after refresh/apply:", getConfig().punctuation);

    if (getConfig().punctuation === false) {
        console.log("REPRODUCED: Punctuation lost after refresh!");
    } else {
        console.log("NOT REPRODUCED: Punctuation retained.");
    }
}

reproduce();

import { apply, __testing } from "../../src/ts/config";

describe("Punctuation retention", () => {
    it("should retain punctuation when applying a config with punctuation: true", async () => {
        const { replaceConfig, getConfig } = __testing;

        // 1. Initial state (default config)
        replaceConfig(getDefaultConfig());
        expect(getConfig().punctuation).toBe(false);

        // 2. Set punctuation to true
        await apply({ punctuation: true }, false);
        expect(getConfig().punctuation).toBe(true);

        // 3. Simulate page refresh/load from local storage
        const savedConfig = { ...getConfig() };
        
        // reset current config to default to simulate fresh start (what happens at the beginning of apply(config, true))
        replaceConfig(getDefaultConfig());
        expect(getConfig().punctuation).toBe(false);

        // Now apply the config we "saved"
        await apply(savedConfig, true);
        expect(getConfig().punctuation).toBe(true);
    });
});
'

+
+import { describe, it, expect } from 'vitest';
+import { getDefaultConfig } from "../../src/ts/constants/default-config";
+import { apply, __testing } from "../../src/ts/config";
+
+describe("Punctuation retention", () => {
+    it("should retain punctuation when applying a config with punctuation: true", async () => {
+        const { replaceConfig, getConfig } = __testing;
+
+        // 1. Initial state (default config)
+        replaceConfig(getDefaultConfig());
+        expect(getConfig().punctuation).toBe(false);
+
+        // 2. Set punctuation to true
+        await apply({ punctuation: true }, false);
+        expect(getConfig().punctuation).toBe(true);
+
+        // 3. Simulate page refresh/load from local storage
+        const savedConfig = { ...getConfig() };
+        
+        // reset current config to default to simulate fresh start (what happens at the beginning of apply(config, true))
+        replaceConfig(getDefaultConfig());
+        expect(getConfig().punctuation).toBe(false);
+
+        // Now apply the config we "saved"
+        await apply(savedConfig, true);
+        expect(getConfig().punctuation).toBe(true);
+    });
+    it("should disable punctuation when switching to quote mode", async () => {
+        const { replaceConfig, getConfig } = __testing;
+        replaceConfig(getDefaultConfig());
+        await apply({ mode: 'time', punctuation: true }, false);
+        expect(getConfig().punctuation).toBe(true);
+
+        // Switch to quote mode
+        await apply({ mode: 'quote' }, false);
+        expect(getConfig().punctuation).toBe(false);
+    });
+
+});

+import { apply, __testing } from "./frontend/src/ts/config";
+import { getDefaultConfig } from "./frontend/src/ts/constants/default-config";
+
+async function reproduce() {
+    const { replaceConfig, getConfig } = __testing;
+
+    // 1. Initial state (default config)
+    replaceConfig(getDefaultConfig());
+    console.log("Initial punctuation:", getConfig().punctuation); // should be false
+
+    // 2. Set punctuation to true
+    // Mimic clicking punctuation button which calls genericSet("punctuation", true)
+    // In our test, we'll use apply to simulate loading from storage or just set it
+    await apply({ punctuation: true }, false);
+    console.log("Punctuation after setting:", getConfig().punctuation); // should be true
+
+    // 3. Simulate page refresh/load from local storage
+    const currentConfig = { ...getConfig() };
+    console.log("Simulating refresh with config:", JSON.stringify({punctuation: currentConfig.punctuation, mode: currentConfig.mode}));
+    
+    // reset current config to default to simulate fresh start
+    replaceConfig(getDefaultConfig());
+    console.log("Config reset. Punctuation:", getConfig().punctuation);
+
+    // Now apply the config we "saved"
+    await apply(currentConfig, true);
+    console.log("Punctuation after refresh/apply:", getConfig().punctuation);
+
+    if (getConfig().punctuation === false) {
+        console.log("REPRODUCED: Punctuation lost after refresh!");
+    } else {
+        console.log("NOT REPRODUCED: Punctuation retained.");
+    }
+}
+
+reproduce();
